                          SIX-A-SIDE FOOTBALL
 R ules
     E x c e p t w h e re o th e r p r o v is io n s in th e s e R u le s are m a d e
 th e ru le s o f A s s o c i a ti o n F o o tb a ll ap p ly . T h e fo llo w in g
 R u le s a re f o r g u id a n c e o nly a n d a r e n o t m a n d a to r y .
     1.     The Laws of the Game of Association Football shall apply
 with the exceptions of Law s 3, 7 and 11.
   u2n u EigL.ht Players m ay be nominated from whom six players
 shall be chosen to form a team. The game shall be played by two
 teams each consisting of not more than six players, one of whom
 shall be the goalkeeper. One of the other players may change
 places with the goalkeeper during the match provided that notice
 is given to the Referee before such change is made.
    7 P urlng a §am e onlY one substitution m a y be m ade.
    4. There will be no offside.
    5. In the event of a match being a draw at full time, it will be
 decided on the basis of the number of corners gained by each
 side If the match is still undecided, play will continue fo r a
further period of six minutes, three minutes each way.
     •      * duration of a 6-a-side game shall not exceed tw o equal
periods of ten minutes, except in circumstances covered by 5
above Allowance may be made in either period for time lost
through accident or other cause, the am ount of which shall be a
m atter for the discretion of the Referee. The interval shall not
exceed five minutes.
        u     Keferee shall be the sole arbiter on points of dispute
and he shal be em powered to interpret the rules governing
6-a-side football, bearing in mind the best interest of all parties
concerned.

                      F IV E -A -S ID E F O O T B A L L
Rules
   Except where other provisions in these rules are m ad e the
rules o f A ssociation Football apply. (E ach rule is num bered
to co rresp o n d with the ap p ro priate Law o f the Game). These
rules are for guidance only and not m a n d ato ry . Five-a-Side
Football m a y be played o r refereed by either men or w om en
Mixed m atches are not permitted.
  244     L A W S FO R S M A L L S I D E M A T C H E S O R C O M P E T I T IO N S



  1.    Playing A rea
      Five-a-Side Football m ay be played in an enclosed area
  indoors or out o f doors. The following dim ensions are
  recom m ended, m axim um length 120' (36 metres) minimum
  100' (30 metres) m axim um width 90' (28 metres) minimum
  6 0' (18.5 metres).
       (a) Centre M ark
    A suitable mark should be made in the exact centre o f the
 playing area on which the ball is dropped to com m ence a
 game. The centre spot should be surrounded bv a circle 3' (1
 metre) in radius.
    ( b) Goal Area
    A semi-circle o f 2 5' (7.5 metres) radius shall be draw n
 from the centre o f each goal line. The extremities o f these
 semi circles should reach the wall or b arricad e regardless of
 whether or not the goal posts encroach on to the field o f play.
    (c) Penalty M ark
    A penalty mark should be placed at a point 20' (6 metres)
 from the centre o f each goal.
    ( d) Goal
    T he goals shall be 16' (5 metres) long by 4' ( 1 2 metres)
 high.

 2.    T he Ball
      The ball used shall be a Five-a-Side ball size four.

 3.     N u m b er o f Players
      (a) T he m a tch shall be played by tw o team s each
 consisting o f n o t m o re th an five players, one o f w h o m shall be
 the goalkeeper.
    (b) O ne substitute per team shall be perm itted at any time
during a game. (Subject to conditions set o u t in the L aw s o f
the G am e)
    (c) A n y o f the other players m a y change places with the
goalkeeper, provided th at the referee is inform ed before the
ch ange is m a d e and provided also th a t the ch ange is m ade
during a stoppage in the game.
   ( d) A m a tch should n o t be considered valid if there are
fewer th a n three players in either o f the teams.
           L A W S F O R S M A L L S I D E M A T C H E S O R C O M P E T IT IO N S   245


  4.     Players’ Equipment
        (a) F o u r players o f th e team shall be dressed in uniform
  shorts an d shirts, goalkeepers m a y w ear track suits b u t the
  colour o f the goalkeepers’ dress m u st be distinguished from
  th a t o f other players, an d the Referee.
    (b) F o o tw e a r
    Light footw ear shall be worn without rigid or hard soles
  bars or studs.

  5.   Referees
     A referee shall be appointed to officiate in each game. He
  shall have the sa m e powers and duties as laid down in the
  Laws o f the G am e.

  6.   Timekeeper/Scorer
     A n independent timekeeper/scorer be appointed to assist
* the referee. T his official shall—
     (a) record goals scored
     (b) ac t as timekeeper an d signify half-time an d full-time by
  an agreed signal
     (c) suspend time on the referee’s instructions for all
  stoppages a n d a d d th a t time to the end o f each half.

  7.    Duration o f the Game
     T he duration o f the gam e shall be tw o equal periods o f six
 minutes, subject to the following:—
     (a) A llow ance shall be m a d e in either period for time lost
 th ro u g h stoppages as decided by the referee and reco rded by
 the timekeeper
     ( b) Time shall be extended to perm it a penalty kick being
 ta k en a t or after the expiration o f the n o rm al period in either
 half. A t half-time the interval shall n o t exceed two minutes
 except by co n sen t o f the referee
       Drawn Games
     In the event o f scores being level at the end o f 12 minutes
 play, extra time o f tw o periods o f tw o minutes m ay be played.
 If the scores are still level after extra time if played, the rules
 o f the competition shall state the method o f ascertaining the
 winners.
246     L A W S FO R S M A L L S I D E M A T C H E S O R C O M PE T IT IO N S



8.     S tart o f Play
      (a) A t the beginning o f a gam e the choice o f ends shall be
decided b y the toss o f a coin.
   (b) P lay shall be started by the referee d ropping the ball on
the centre spot between one player from each side, each o f
w hom shall stand n o t less th a n 3' (1 metre) from the centre
m ark.
   (c) T he gam e shall be re-started in like m a n n er after a goal
has been scored.
   (id) After an y other stoppage the gam e shall be re-started
by the referee dropping the ball a t a point n earest to w here it
w as when play w as suspended, unless it w as in the
goalkeeper’s possession, w hen the player shall, at the referee’s
signal, roll the ball o u t to re-start the game.
   The referee shall not drop the ball within 6' (2 metres) of
the lines marking the goal areas or within 6' o f surrounding
walls or barricades.

9.   Ball In an d O ut o f Play
  T he ball shall be in play at all times from the start o f the
game unless:—
  (a) the ball rises ab ove h ead height
  (b) the ball has crossed the goal-line or the barricades
surrounding the playing area
  (c) the timekeeper h as given the signal for h alf or full-time
  ( d) the gam e h as been stopped by the referee
     Ball above Head Height
  The ball m ust be kept below head height. (The referee shall
have discretion as to w hat constitutes ‘head height’) The
heading o f the ball is allowed provided the aforementioned
condition is observed.
      Penalty fo r infringement.
   Indirect free-kick at the place where the ball was last
played (unless the ball was last played by the ‘defending
goalkeeper in the goal area, in which case the indirect free-
kick shall be tak en from a point n o t less th a n 6' (2 metres)
outside the goal a re a n earest to w here the offence occurred.
   If the ball rebounds to above head height from any o f the
following situations,
   (i) F ro m a player who has m ad e no attem pt to play the ball
           L A W S FO R S M A L L S I D E M A T C H E S O R C O M P E T IT IO N S   247



    (ii) F ro m a wall, barricade, goalpost, crossbar or other
 obstruction
 then the referee will re-start the play by dropping the ball at
 the point w here the reb o u n d occurred. (If this point is within
 the goal area the ball shall be d ropped at a point not less than
 6 (2 metres) outside the goal area nearest to where the
 rebound occurred)
       B all out o f Play
    W hen the ball goes out o f play but below head height a
 m em ber o f the opposing team shall roll the ball into play
 W hen m em ber o f the defending team puts the ball o u t o f play
 over the barricade on th a t p la y er’s own goal-line but below
 h ead height, the opposing team shall be aw arded a roll-in
 corner. W hen a m em ber o f the attacking team puts the ball
 out o f play over the b arricad e on the o p p o n en ts’ goal-line, but
 below head height, the goalkeeper shall roll the ball out (If
 the ball drops on the back o f the net behind the goal, it shall
 be regarded as out o f play and the gam e shall be restarted
 with a roll-out by the goalkeeper)

 10.      Scoring
    A goal is scored w hen the whole o f the ball crosses the
goal-line between the goal posts and under the crossbar
provided it has not been throw n, carried or propelled by h an d
or arm by a player o f the attacking side, except in the case o f
a goalkeeper, who is within his own goal area.
    A goal is not allowed if the ball was last played by a player
o f the attacking side whilst within either goal area. (If the ball
is last played by a defending player whilst within either goal
area, a goal shall be allowed, unless th a t player entered the
goal area accidentally.)

11.      Offside
   T here is no offside. Players m ay place themselves in any
p art o f the playing area outside the goal areas.

12. Fouls and Misconduct
  (a)  Charging is forbidden an d shall be penalised by the
aw arding o f a direct free-kick.
248   L A W S FOR S M A L L S I D E M A T C H E S O R C O M PE T IT IO N S



    (b)    A player who intentionally obstructs an o p ponent when
n o t playing the ball shall be penalised b y th e aw ard o f an
indirect free-kick.
   A player who is sent off shall not be allowed to take any
further p a rt in the competition on that day, nor in subsequent
rounds until permission is given by the C om m ittee governing
the Com petition. T he referee m ust report cases o f misconduct
within 2 days (Sundays not included) to the Sanctioning
Association.
   N o substitute is allowed for a player dismissed from the
playing area for misconduct during the gam e in which the
offence occurred, but a substitute m ay be played in any
ensuing games.
 13. Free-Kick
   W hen a player is taking a direct or indirect free-kick, all of
the opposing players shall be at least 6' (2 metres) from the
ball until it is in play.
   All free-kicks (except penalty kicks) given against the
defending side for infringements com m itted in or near the
goal area, shall be taken from a distance o f not less than 6' (2
metres) outside the goal area at the nearest point to where the
offence occurred.
14.    Penalty-Kick
   A penalty kick shall be taken from the penalty m ark and
except for the defending goalkeeper, only the player taking
the kick can enter the goal area and for th at p urpose only.
   W hether or not a goal is scored from the kick, the player
concerned m ust leave the goal area im mediately and before
taking any further part in play.
15.    Goalkeeper Returning the Ball into Play
   After holding the ball the goalkeeper m ust immediately
return the ball into play with an u n d erarm bowling action. It
m ust not be throw n nor kicked and it m ust be kept below
head height.
  Penalty fo r Infringement
  An indirect free-kick shall be taken by a player o f the
opposing team from a spot 6' (2 metres) outside the goal area
nearest to where the infringement occurred.
            LAWS FOR SMALL SIDE MATCHES OR COMPETITIONS           24 9


 16. Play Within the Goal Area
   (a) Only the defending goalkeeper is allowed within the
      1f r?a’ff xce.pt whe” ,a Penalty kick has been awarded and
then only the player taking the kick can enter the goal area.
   If a goalkeeper leaves the goal area he is then treated as
any other player.
Penalty f o r Infringem ent
           th? a tta c k ~ ~ a direct free-kick at the point o f entry
 into the goal area                                                  y
    (ii) By the defence-— a penalty kick
    N ote: Referees should distinguish between accidental and
intentional entry into or exit from the goal area. Only
deliberate actions w here the player either plays the ball or
tries to play the ball should be penalised. Accidental entry or
exit which has no effect on the play should be ignored.

17.   Throw-Ins, Goal Kicks, Corner Kicks
  T here are no goal kicks, corners o r throw-ins.

 17.    Suspension of Game and Extension of Season
      The Council shall have pow er to suspend the game either sectionally or entirely.
      They may also ex tend th e periods for playing, as from tim e to time, in the n
 discretion, shall be dee med necessary, or desirable, and agreements between Clubs
 Players, and Officials shall be subject to such decisions.
 18.    Players with Written Contracts
 (a)    Minimum Age
       No Player who is und er th e age of eighteen (18) years and w ho is receiving full-time
 education in acco rd an ce with th e Education Acts shall en ter into a contract of em plo y­
 m e nt with a Club in membership with The Association or an affiliated Association but
 he may be registered as an Associated Schoolboy.
       No Player w h o is und er th e age o f seventeen (17) years shall enter into a co ntract
 of em plo ym e nt with a Club in Membership with The Association or an affiliated
 Association, except as a Trainee as provided by Rule 20.
 (bi    Financial Arrangem ents — Registration
      Subject to paragraph (a) of this Rule, and t o the Rules and Regulations of th e
 League of which th e Club is a Member, any Club in Membership with The Association or
 an affiliated Association may negotiate whatever financial arrangements with its Players
 as may be mutually acceptable. All Players under w ritten co n tract mus t be registered
 with The Association.
 (c)   Co ntract o f E m plo ym ent
      All co ntracts of em p lo ym ent o r letters of em plo y m en t exchanged between a Club
and any Official, Player, Manager, Coach, Trainer o r any oth e r employee of the Club,
shall specify th a t all em olu ments due to the individual shall be paid to the individual
co ncerned and not to any com pany or agency acting on behalf of th e employee, and all
such contracts shall specify th a t th e individual is directly un der th e disciplinary control
of th e Club and of The Association. No pay m en t in respect of th e registration or transfer
of registration shall be made to an agent.
 (d)   Form " G (1 ) " -R e g i s t r a ti o n for One (1) Calendar Month
      A Player who desires to be registered with The Association f o r a period of one (1)
ca lendar m onth m u st sign th e form marked "G (1 )" in the Schedule annexed to these
Rules.           *
 (f)   Forms to be return ed t o The Association
        The Forms men tion ed in paragraphs (d) and (e) above m ust be returned to the
Secretary of The Association within five (5) days of being signed by th e Player and
accom panied by a co p y of th e contract.
       A Player seeking registration under written con tract shall no t be allowed to play
u n d er th e terms of th e contract until th e Club registering him shall have received his
registration certificate from The Association.

(j)    Agreements be tween Clubs and Players
       Clubs must enter into a written contract with their Players in th e form, or sub­
stantially th e form, approved by The Association and known as 'Form of Agreement'
with or w ithou t including th e opti on hereinafter mentioned. Such co ntracts of em ploy­
ment which mus t be signed at the same time as th e registration form may be for any
period of time which shall be clearly stated in the con tract of em plo y m en t but shall
cover th e same pe riod as th e registration and contain all th e terms and conditions of
em p lo ym e n t before being signed. A co p y of th e contract of em plo ym e nt m u st be handed
to th e Player at the ti me of signing.

the Secretary/M anager/Chairm an o f and acting pursuant to Resolution and

Football Club Limited (hereinafter referred to as “ the Club”) o f the one part and
(nam e)..............................................................................................................................................
o f (address)................................................................................... ..................................................

a Registered A ssociation Football Player (hereinafter referred to as “the Player")

W H ER EB Y it is agreed as follows:—
    1. This Agreement shall remain in force until the 30th day o f June 19......................
unless it shall have previously been terminated by substitution o f a revised agreement
or as hereinafter provided.
    2. The Player agrees to play to the best o f his ability in all football matches in
which he is selected to play for the Club and to attend at any reasonable place for the
purpose o f training in accordance with instructions given by any duly authorised
official o f the Club.
   3. The Player agrees to attend all matches in which the Club is engaged when
directed by any duly authorised official o f the Club.
   4. The Player shall play football solely for the Club or as authorised by the Club
or as required under the Rules and Regulations o f the Football Association and the
Football League. The Player undertakes to adhere to the Laws o f the G am e of
Association Football in all matches in which he participates.
    5. The Player agrees to observe the Rules o f the Club at all times. The Club and
the Player shall observe and be subject to the Rules and Regulations o f the Football
Association and the Football League. In the case o f conflict such Rules and
 Regulations shall take precedence over this Agreement and over the Rules o f the
 Club.
    6. The Club undertakes to provide the Player at the earliest opportunity with
copies o f all relevant Football Association Rules, Football League Regulations, the
Club Rules for players and any relevant insurance policy applicable to the Player
and to provide him with any subsequent amendments to all the above.
   7. The Player shall not without the written consent o f the Club participate
professionally in any other sporting or athletic activity. The Player shall at all times
have due regard for the necessity of his maintaining a high standard o f physical
fitness and agrees not to indulge in any sport, activity or practice that might
endanger such fitness. The Player shall not infringe any provision in this regard in
any policy o f insurance taken out for his benefit or for the benefit o f the Club.
   8. A ny incapacity or sickness shall be reported by the Player to the Club
immediately and the Club shall keep a record o f any incapacity. The Player shall
submit promptly to such medical and dental examinations as the Club may
reasonably require and shall undergo, at no expense to himself, such treatment as
may be prescribed by the medical or dental advisers o f the Club in order to restore
the Player to fitness. The Club shall arrange promptly such prescribed treatment and
shall ensure that such treatment is undertaken and completed without expense to the
                         FO R M S O F T H E A S S O C IA T IO N                   263


Player notwithstanding that this Agreement expires after such treatm ent has been
prescribed.
    9.    Subject to the provisions of Clause 10, in the event that the Player shall
becom e incapacitated by reason of sickness or injury the Club shall, unless provision
for the continuation of bonus payments be set out in the Schedule to this A greem ent
during the period o f incapacity, pay to the Player for the first twenty-eight w eeks of
incapacity his basic wage as specified in the Schedule plus a sum equivalent to the
am oun t o f sickness benefit which the C lub is able to recoup.
   A fte r twenty-eight weeks o f incapacity the Club shall, unless provision for the
continuation o f bonus paym ents be set o ut in the Schedule to this A greem ent pay to
the Player his basic wage as specified in the Schedule w ithout reduction for any state
sickness or injury benefit that he may receive.
    The provisions o f this Clause apply only to the playing season.
    The Player agrees to notify the Club of any sickness benefit received after the end
o f the playing season in order for the Club to deduct the am ount from the Player’s
gross wage.
  10. In the event that the Player shall suffer permanent incapacity the Club shall be
entitled to serve a notice upon the Player terminating the Agreement. The Player’s
minimum entitlement shall be to receive 6 m onths’ notice where the Agreement has
not more than 3 years to run with an extra m onth’s notice for each year or part year
in excess o f the said 3 years, provided that the parties shall be able to negotiate a
longer period o f notice if they so wish.
   The notice may be served at any time after:—
   (a) the date on which the Player is declared permanently totally disabled in a
case where the Player suffers incapacity within the terms o f the Football League
Personal Accident Insurance Scheme; or
   (b) in any other case, the date on which the incapacity is established by
independent medical examination.
  11. (a) The Player shall not reside at any place which the Club deems unsuitable
for the performance o f his duties under this Agreement.
   (b) The Player shall not without the previous consent o f the Club be engaged
either directly or indirectly in any trade, business or occupation other than his
employment hereunder.
 12. The Player shall be given every opportunity compatible with his obligations
under this Agreement to follow courses o f further education or vocational training if
he so desires. The Club agrees to give the Footballers’ Further Education and
Vocational Training Society particulars o f any such courses undertaken by the
Player.
  13. The Player shall permit the Club to photograph him as a member o f the squad
o f players and staff o f the Club provided that such photographs are for use only as
the official photographs o f the Club. The Players may, save as otherwise mutually
agreed and subject to the overriding obligation contained in the Rules o f the Football
Association not to bring the game o f Association Football into disrepute, contribute
to the public media in a responsible manner. The Player shall, whenever
circumstances permit, give to the Club reasonable notice o f his intention to make
such contributions to the public media in order to allow representation to be m ade to
him on behalf o f the Club if it so desires,
  14. (a) The Player shall not induce or attempt to induce any other Player
employed by or registered by the Club, or by any other Football League Club, to
leave that employment or cease to be so registered for any reason whatsoever.
 264                     fo rm s    o f t h e a s s o c ia t io n



      (b)     The Club and the Player shall arrange all contracts o f service and transfers
  o f registration to any other Football Club between themselves and shall m ake no
  paym ent to any other person or agent in this respect.

    15. N o payment shall be made or received by either the Player or the Club to or
  from any person or organisation whatsoever as an inducement to win, lose or draw a
  match except for such payments to be made by the Club to the Player as are
  specifically provided for in the Schedule to this Agreement.

    16. If the Player shall be guilty o f serious or persistent misconduct or serious or
  persistent breach o f the Rules o f the Club or o f the terms and conditions of this
  Agreement the Club may on giving fourteen days’ notice to the Player terminate this
  Agreement in accordance with the Rules o f the Football Association and the
  Regulations o f the Football League and the Club shall notify the Player in writing of
  the full reasons for the action taken. Such action shall be subject to the Player’s right
 o f appeal (exercisable within seven days of the receipt by the Player o f such notice
 and notification o f reasons from the Club) as follows:—
     (a) he m ay appeal to the Management Committee who shall hear the appeal
 within fourteen days o f receipt of the notice o f appeal.
     (b) either the Club or the Player m ay appeal against the decision o f the
 M anagement Committee to the Football League Appeals Committee and such
 further appeal shall be m ade within seven days o f the receipt o f the Management
 C ommittee’s decision and shall be heard within fourteen days o f receipt o f the notice
 o f the further appeal.
     Any such termination shall be subject to the rights o f the parties provided for in
 the Regulations o f the Football League. The Club m ay at its discretion waive its
 rights under this Clause and take action under the provisions o f Clause 18.
  17. If the Club is guilty o f serious or persistent breach o f the terms and conditions
o f this Agreement the Player m ay on giving fourteen days’ written notice to the Club
terminate this Agreement. The Player shall forward a copy o f such notice to the
Football League and to the Football Association. The Club shall have a right of
appeal as set out in Clause 16(a) mutatis mutandis (exercisable within seven days of
the receipt by the Club o f such notice from the Player) and the Club o r the Player as
the case m ay be shall have a further right o f appeal as set out in Clause 16(b).
   18. If the Player is guilty o f misconduct or a breach o f any o f the training or
 disciplinary rules or lawful instructions o f the Club or any of the provisions o f this
 Agreement the Club may either impose a fine not exceeding two weeks’ basic wages
or order the Player not to attend at the Club for a period not exceeding fourteen
days. The Club shall inform the Player in writing o f the action taken and the full
reasons for it and this information shall be recorded in a register held at the Club
The Player shall have a right o f appeal as set out in Clause 16(a) (exercisable within
seven days o f the receipt by the Player o f such written notification from the Club)
and the Club or the Player as the case m ay be shall have a further right o f appeal as
set out in Clause 16(b) of this Agreement. Any penalty imposed by the Club upon
the Player shall not become operative until the appeals procedures have been
exhausted.
 19. In the event o f any grievance in connection with his employment under this
Agreement the following procedures shall be available to the Player in the order set
out:—
  (a)      the grievance shall be brought informally to the notice o f the M anager o f the
Club in the first instance,
                               FO R M S O F T H E A S S O C IA T IO N

  c ) (b)   formal notice o f the grievance m ay be given in writing to the M anager o f the

  infringe any provision in this regard in any Policy o f Insurance taken out for his

  may render such insurance void or voidable.
      8. (a) A ny incapacity or sickness shall be reported by the Player to the Club
  immediately and if this employment is or becomes the Player’s primary
  employment*.—
      (i) he must notify the Club o f his expected date o f return and if the Player is
  unable to attend the Club for training or matches due to sickness or injury for any
  period exceeding 3 days the Player must complete a self certification form for the
  payment o f his salary during illness.                *
      (ii) if the Player’s incapacity continues for m ore than 7 days (including
  weekends) the Player must obtain a certificate from a registered Practitioner or
  Hospital and send it to the Club without delay. If requested by the Club the Player
  must send a Medical Certificate for each week o f absence thereafter.
     (b)      The Player shall submit promptly to such medical and/or dental
 examinations as the Club may reasonably require and shall submit to such treatment
 as m ay be prescribed and provided by the medical a nd /or dental advisers to the
 Club. The Club shall arrange promptly such prescribed treatment and shall ensure
 that such treatment is undertaken and completed.
     9. Subject to the provisions o f Clause 10, in the event that the Player shall
 become incapacitated by reason o f injury sustained whilst playing o r training for the
 Club or sickness the Club shall, unless special provision be set out in the Schedule to
 this Agreement, during the period o f incapacity pay to the Player his basic wage as
 specified in the Schedule. In the event that the Player shall become so injured, other
 than whilst playing or training for the Club, then unless this employmenmt is or
 becomes the Player’s primary employment it shall be in the discretion o f the Club
 after a period o f two weeks from the date the injury was sustained as to whether or
 not to pay the Player his basic wage until such time as he is able to train fully with
 the rest o f the C lub’s Players.
     10. In the event that the Player shall suffer permanent incapacity in any
 circumstances, then the Club shall be entitled to serve notice upon the Player
 terminating this Agreement. The Player’s minimum entitlement shall be to receive
 three months notice where the Agreement has not more than 3 years to run with an
 extra m onth s notice for each year or part year in excess o f the said three years.
 Provided that the parties shall be able to negotiate a longer period o f notice if they so
 wish or reach a mutually agreed settlement. Such notice may be served at any time
 after (a) the date on which the Player is declared permanently incapacitated in a case
where the Player suffers incapacity within the terms o f a League personal accident
insurance scheme; or (b) in any other case, the date on which the permanent
incapacity is established by independent medical examination.
     11. The Player shall not engage in any business or reside at any place other than
that agreed a t the date o f this Agreement which the Club reasonably deems
unsuitable for the performance o f his duties under this Agreement.
     12. If this employment is or becomes the Player’s primary employment and:—
    (a) the Player is retained by the Club at the end o f the playing season then the
Player shall be entitled to four weeks holiday during the close season, and
    (b) the Player shall be given every opportunity compatible with his obligations
under this Agreement to follow courses o f further education or vocational training if
he so desires.
    13. The Player shall permit the Club to photograph him as a member o f the
squad o f players a nd /or staff o f the Club provided that such photographs are for use

right o f appeal as set out in Clause 16(a) mutatis mutandis (exercisable within 7 days
o f the receipt by the Player o f such notice from the Club) and the Club or the Player
as the case may be shall have a further right o f appeal as set out in clause 16(b).
     Any penalty imposed by the Club upon the Player shall not be operative until the
appeals procedure has been completely exhausted.
     19. In the event o f any grievance in connection with his employment under this
Agreement the following procedure shall be available to the Player in the order set
out:—
     (a) the grievance shall be brought informally to the notice o f the M anager o f the
Club in the first instance
     (b) formal notice o f the grievance may be given in writing to the M anager o f the
Club
     (c) if the grievance is not settled to the Player’s satisfaction within 14 days
 thereafter formal notice o f the grievance may be given in writing to the Secretary o f
 the Club so that it may be considered by the board o f Directors o r Committee o f the
 Club o r by any duly authorised committee or sub-committee thereof. The matter
 shall thereupon be dealt with by the Board or Committee at its next convenient
 meeting and in any event within four weeks o f receipt o f the notice
     (d) if the grievance is not settled by the Club to the Player’s satisfaction the
 Player shall have the right o f appeal as set out in Clause 16(a) (exercisable within 7
 days o f the Club notifying the Player o f the decision o f the Board or Committee) and
 the Club or the Player as the case may be shall have a further right o f appeal as set
 out in clause 16(b) o f this Agreement.
      20. The Player may if he so desires be represented at any personal hearing of
  any appeal under this Agreement by an official or member o f the Professional
  Footballers’ Association.
      21. This Agreement may be terminated at any time by mutual consent o f both
  the Club and the Player.
      22. Upon the execution o f this Agreement the Club shall effect the Registration
  o f the Player with The Association and the League(s) o f which the Club is a member
  in accordance with their Rules. Such registration may be transferred by mutual
  consent o f the Club and the Player during the currency o f this Agreement and this
  Agreement will be deemed to be terminated on the registration by The Association o f
  such transfer.
      23. As agreed in Clause 1 this Agreement (subject to the Rules o f The
  Association) shall cease and terminate on the first Saturday in M ay or the date o f the
  last League or Cup match o f the Club’s first team whichever is the later unless
  either:—
      (a) this Agreement shall have previously been determined in accordance with the
   provisions o f one or other o f Clause 16, 17,21 or 22 hereinbefore set forth; or
      (b) the Club shall have, on or before the first Saturday in M ay or the date o f the
   last League or Cup match o f the Club’s first team whichever is the later by notice in
   writing to the Player (by registered or recorded post or a written acknowledgement
   being otherwise obtained) and to The Association indicated that the Club either
   offers a further re-engagement to the Player o r if appropriate exercises the option
   contained in the Schedule hereto.
       (i)    I f the notice offers re-engagement the notice shall specify the terms and
   conditions which the Club is prepared to agree shall apply during the period of
   re-engagement. Such terms and conditions must be the same or not less favourable
   overall than those which applied during the initial period o f employment or the
   option period (if applicable). The Player M UST notify in writing the Club holding his
                          FORMS OF THE ASSOCIATION                                 271


   registration within twenty eight days of receipt of the said notice whether or not he
   accepts its ofTer of re-engagement. IF THE PLAYER HAS NOT REPLIED in
   writing to the Club’s ofTer of re-engagement within the time limit then the ofTer shall
   automatically lapse and the Club’s compensation rights shall not be afTected and the
  existing Agreement shall be deemed to continue for the further period of
  re-engagement specified in the notice by the Club and on the terms and conditions of
  the existing Agreement save for any option provision. If within the period of twenty
  eight days of receipt of the notice by the Club making the ofTer the Player notifies the
  Club that he does not accept the ofTer and thereafter the Player and the Club do not
  agree any other terms and conditions and sign an Agreement embodying the same or
  if within the said period of twenty eight days terms for the transfer of the Player to
  another Club have not been agreed both the Club and the Player shall have the right
  to refer the matter to the Management Committee of the more Senior League of
  which the Club is a Member for decision in respect of both financial terms and
  conditions offered or transfer fee imposed provided that if either the Club or the
  Player is dissatisfied with the decision of the League each shall be entitled to appeal
  to the League Appeals Committee by notice in writing of an appeal delivered to The
  Association within twenty eight days of the receipt by the Club or the Player
  respectively of the decision of the Management Committee of the League Until
  another Contract of Service between the Club and the Player becomes operative or
 the registration of the Player is transferred either prior to or as a result of the
 determination of an appeal from either the Club or the Player, the Player’s Contract
 of Service shall, after the Club shall have served notice on him be deemed to continue
 and have full force and efTect between the parties thereto on the like terms and
 conditions as those pertaining prior to the expiration of the initial period of
 employment or the option period, if appropriate, and the Player will continue to train
 and play as instructed by the Club.
      (ii)    If the notice exercises the option contained in the Schedule hereto on the
 same or not less favourable terms and conditions overall as in this Agreement but
 excluding the option provision and so that such further period (herein called ‘the
 option period’) shall not be for longer in extent than that of the initial period of
 employment then this Agreement shall continue in full force and efTect, save and
 except paragraph (c) of the Schedule, as between the parties hereto and shall
 terminate on the last day of the option period unless either:—
     this Agreement shall have been determined previously in accordance with the
    provisions of one or other of clauses 16, 17, 21 or 22 hereinbefore set forth; or
    the Club shall have offered a period of re-engagement to the Player in accordance
    with the provisions of sub-clause (b)(i) hereof as if the same were here set out
    mutatis mutandis.
     (lii) In the event of the option contained in the Schedule hereto being exercised or
an ofTer of re-engagement being made in accordance with this Clause the Club and
Player may agree for a basic wage to continue to be paid during the close season as
provided for in paragraph (d) in the Schedule to this Agreement.
    24. The remuneration of the Player shall be set out in the Schedule attached to
this Agreement and signed by the parties. The Schedule shall include all
remuneration to which the Player is or may be entitled. In the event of any dispute
the remuneration set out in the Schedule shall be conclusively deemed to be the full
entitlement of the Player.
    25. Reference herein to Rules of the Leagues of which the Club is a member.
The Association, the Club and any other body shall be treated as a reference to those
Rules as from time to time amended.

  26. All Previous Agreements between the Club and the Player are hereby
cancelled.
  27. All notices required to be given by the provision of this Agreement shall be
so given, unless otherwise provided herein, by first class prepaid post to the last
known address of the addressee.

TR AIN EES

20. A Player betw een his fifteenth (1 5 th ) and seventeenth (1 7 th ) birthdays who is not receiving full­
time education in accordance with the Education Acts m ay be registered as a Trainee with The Association.
The period o f a registration will be made on the form m arked “ G (3)” in the Schedule annexed to these
Rules and will be for a m axim um period o f two (2 ) calander years.

      On or a fte r his seventeenth (1 7 th ) birthday he may sign as a Player under w ritten contract subject
to the Rules and Regulations o f the League or Com bination o f which th e Club is a m em ber, and to the
general Rules o f The Association with reference to Players under w ritten contract or remain as a Trainee.

       If a Player wishes to becom e a Player under written contract, the Club for which he was registered
as a T rainee shall be entitled to his registration as a Player under w ritten contract. If the Club does not
wish to register the Player he shall be free to register for any o th er Club.

      E ach form , after com pletion o f all particulars, including dates and signature, m ust be signed b y the
Player, attested b y his parent or guardian and returned to the Secretary o f The Association within five (5)
days o f such signature, accom panied b y a copy o f the agreement entered into b y the Club and the Player
and also a c opy o f his certificate o f b irth. The wages to b e paid m ust be set out in the schedule o f the
agreement and will be a t the rate laid dow n by the Y outh Training Scheme.

      A Trainee does n o t becom e a m em ber o f a Club no r is he allowed to play until the Club registering
him shall have received acknowledgem ent o f the registration from The Association.

      T he nam es o f such Players shall be published and no Club no r any person shall attem p t to induce
such a Player to leave the Club for which he is registered.

A P la y e r w h o is re g iste re d a s a T ra i n e e m ay p la y fo r a n o t h e r C l u b , s u b je c t to the w ritte n a p p r o v a l o f
t h e C l u b fo r w h ich he is r e g iste re d . A c o p y o f the w r itte n p e r m is s io n m u s t b e given to th is
A s s o c i a ti o n , the L e ag u e o r C o m b in a t io n o f w h ic h th e C lu b is a M e m b e r , th e P la y e r a n d th e C lu b fo r
 w h ich he is t o play.

      A Player who is registered as a Trainee may apply to his Club for the cancellation of his registration
during th e m axim um period o f two (2 ) years. In such circum stances, he m ay n o t subsequently sign as a
Trainee or as a Player under w ritten contract for a Club until a fter a laspe o f two (2 ) years except with
the consent o f the Q u b fo r which he was registered as a Trainee.

     At the request o f the Player or his parent, the Club shall allow the Player to continue his further
education or take up suitable vocational training.

       If a Club fails to fulfil this obligation o r its agreement the Player shall be entitled to apply to his
Club fo r the cancellation o f his registration or to sign as a Trainee fo r an o th e r Club. A P layer shall have
the right o f appeal to the Management Com mittee o f the League o r Com bination o f which the Club is in
M embership if his application b e unreasonably withheld. If either party is dissatisfied with a decision there
shall be a furthe r right o f appeal in accordance with the sanctioned Rules o f the C om petion concerned.

        The provisions o f Rule 18 (1) and 18 (m ) shall apply in the case o f Trainees.

           18. (g) Transfers
              The registration of a Player may be transferred from one Club to another on the
           form marked “H” in the schedule annexed to these Rules, The Council require to be
           satisfied that the transfer of registration is bona fide and applications for the purpose
           of obtaining Players’ registrations for special matches will not be acceded to. In the
           event of a transfer of registration the Player must be re-registered by the Club to
           which his registration is transferred. If it is desired to register a Player or transfer his
           registration at the last possible moment, the registration form, contract of
           employment and the transfer form (if any) must be sent by first class post and either
           a tele-message addressed “Football Association, London W2 3LW”, or a telex,
           intimating the time of posting sent to the Secretary of The Association, in which case
           the forms, if in order, shall be regarded as received at the time intimated on the
            tele-message or telex. The forms may also be sent by facsimile copying machine to the
            Offices of The Association and, if in order, will be regarded as received at the time of
           receipt.
               Subject to clause (1) of this rule, the Council shall have the power to cancel the
            registration of a Player at any time upon application of the Player, or of his Club,

                             APPENDIX
               REGULATIONS OF THE F.I.F.A.
(Approved and adopted by Congress 1953 and altered by subsequent
                         Congresses.)



                          I. Qualification of Players

Article 1
R E C O G N IT IO N O F Q U A L IFIC A T IO N S
Each National Association shall determine the status and qualifications ot
its players, and the Federation and all affiliated Associations shall recog­
nize such qualifications.

Article 2
S O U R C E O F PR O F IT
Whatever may be the status of its players, a club, in order to be affiliated to
one of the Associations of the Federation, shall not be used as a source of
profit to its directors o r shareholders. Nevertheless, in regard to the latter,
the payment of a normal rate of interest is permissible.



                             II. Definition of Matches

 Article 3
 IN T E R N A T IO N A L M A TC H A
 1. An International Football Match A officially recognized by the Federa­
    tion and subject to the provisions of Art. 37 of the Statutes shall be a
    match arranged between two National Associations who are members
    of the Federation and in which the home country fields its first national
      representative team.
 IN T E R N A T IO N A L M A TC H B
 2. An International Football Match B officially recognized by the Federa­
    tion shall be a match arranged between two National Associations who
    are members of the Federation and in which the home country fields
    another team than its first national representative team.
  D E SIG N A T IO N A N D T ITLE
  3 The designation and title of the match must be that recognized politi­
     cally and geographically of the countries o r territories of the National
     Associations playing the match and over which they have sole control
      and jurisdiction.
                                  AP PENDIX                               285


N A T IO N A L IT Y O F PL A Y E R S
4. Every player who is a citizen of a country by virtue of the laws of the
   country is qualified to play in international o r representative teams for
   that country.
5. When a player has played in an international or representative match
   for the country for which he is qualified in accordance with para. 4, he
   shall not be eligible to play in such matches for any other country.
6. The only exceptions to the requirements of paras. 4 and 5 would be
   when the nationality of a player has been changed, not voluntarily, but
   by an international decision giving independence to a country or
   making provision for the detachment of a region o r part of a country
   and which thereby becomes part of another country.
7. If a National Association allows one of its Leagues to select a team to
   represent its country, the match shall be recognized as an International
   M atch and be governed by the provisions o f A rt. 6.
8. A n International Match between two affiliated National Associations
   shall not be officially recorded as such if, prior to the date o f the match,
   one o f the A ssociations has expressed a wish to this effect to both the
   Federation and the other A ssociation concerned, but the levy due to the
   Federation under Art. 37 of the Statutes shall nevertheless be due in
   respect of such a match.


Article 4
IN T E R -L E A G U E M A TC H ES
A n Inter-League match shall be a match played between two Leagues; and
although the Leagues may belong to different National Associations the
match shall not be recognized as an International Match.


Article 5
IN T E R -C L U B M A TCH ES
1. A n Inter-Club match shall be a match played between two clubs, and
   although the clubs concerned may belong to different National Associ­
   ations such a match shall not be recognized as an International Match.
   (Inter-Club matches between clubs of the same nationality shall not be
   governed by the Regulations of the Federation.)
2. Matches between teams o f different nationalities which are not defined
   as International Matches under Art. 3 and 4 must not be played without
   the express permission of the National A ssociations concerned.
286                             APPENDIX


                        III.   International Matches
Article 6
N O TIF IC A T IO N TO T H E F.I.F.A.
1. National Associations must give notice of International Matches A and
   B (Art. 3, paras. 1 and 2) to the Federation within 14 days of being
   arranged, and such notification must reach the Federation at least 48
   hours before the date of the match.
FINES
2. For matches not notified in accordance with section 1, a fine of 50 Swiss
   Francs shall be inflicted by the Federation. For matches which are not
   notified at all the fine shall be 100 Swiss Francs. These fines must be
   paid within 7 days of receiving the decision o f the Federation.
REPORT
3. Within 14 days of the playing of each International Match, A o r B, the
   Secretary of the National Association within whose jurisdiction the
   ground is situated shall furnish the following information to the office
   o f the Secretary of the Federation on theofficial form of the Federation:
   result o f the match; names of the referee and linesmen; the surname and
   Christian name of each of the players, and o f substitutes of both teams,
   and the status of the players. The official form must be completed and
   signed. If this regulation is not observed, a fine of 50 Swiss Francs shall
      be imposed.
 4. For each week o r part of a week that the above report is late, o r if it is
    incomplete, a fine of 50 Swiss Francs, payable within 7 days of receiv­
    ing the decision of the Federation, shall be imposed. In the event of a
    second offence, the Executive Committee may increase the fines.

 Article 7
 REFEREES
 1. In International Matches, the referee selected must belong to a neutral
    country except when the two National A ssociations concerned have
    reached a mutual agreement previously.
 2. T he referee so selected must be from the official List of International
      Referees.
                        IV. Inter-League Matches
 Article 8
 APPROV AL
 1. Inter-League matches between teams of different National Associa­
    tions must be previously approved by the National Associations con­
    cerned.




                                                                                   •N
                                APPENDIX                                287


2. Each League must observe the Status and Regulations of its own
National Association.


                         V. Inter-Club Matches
Article 9
C O N SEN T
1. Matches between clubs belonging to different National Associations
   shall not be played without the express consent of the National Associ­
   ations concerned. National A ssociations must include in their Regula­
   tions a time limit within which clubs must make their applications for
   permission and lay down the penalties for infringements.
2. A frontier club may, with the consent of the two National Associations
   concerned, play another frontier club by giving at least 24 hours notice,
   o r the notice stipulated by the Regulations of the two National Associa­
   tions concerned.
3. A National Association must inform the other National Association
   concerned of any matches known to have been arranged o r played
   under its jurisdiction and for which prior consent has not been
   obtained.
4. Scratch teams consisting of players not belonging to the same club or
   Association shall not play clubs o r team s representing A ssociations or
   N ations except with the consent of all the competing teams and of the
   National A ssociations concerned and of the Federation.
5. The consent of the Federation is obligatory for any tournam ent in
   which more than three teams of different National A ssociations take
   part. In addition, the Regulations governing the tournam ent must be
   sent to the Secretariat of the Federation for approval.


      VI. Restrictions Regarding the Arrangement o f Matches and
                          Transfer o f Players
Article 10
F O R B ID D E N SP O N S O R IN G
1. The employment o f agents or intermediaries in the transfer o f players is
   strictly forbidden,
2. If the Statutes and Regulations of a National Association do not
   include an Article forbidding:
A G EN TS
   (a) The employment of intermediaries in the transfer of players
288                              APPENDIX


   (b) The playing of matches arranged by private individuals for the
        purpose of profit
  It m ust insert in its Statutes an Article reproducing the text of the present
Art. 10.
3. Unless the Statutes o r Regulations of a National Association specifi­
    cally forbid the employment of agents o r intermediaries for the
    arrangement o f matches, then it is not forbidden. The F.I.F.A., how­
    ever, can only intervene to enforce the carrying out of agreements made,
    if the following conditions with regard to tHe organization of matches
    are observed:
   (a) F or matches between teams belonging to the same Continental
         Confederation the agent o r intermediary must be officially recog­
         nized by the Continental Confederation concerned.
   (b) F or matches between teams belonging to different Continental
          Confederations the agent o r intermediary must be officially recog­
          nized by F.I.F.A. and have given F.I.F.A. a bank guarantee of
         $25,000. A list of recognized agents or intermediaries will be
          published by F.I.F.A. and the Continental Confederations.
CONTRACT
   (c) Agreements made either with agents o r intermediaries o r by the
         latter with an Association o r Club, m ust be set out in writing, in
         duplicate, in the form of a binding contract signed by both parties.
C O N FIR M IN W R ITIN G
   (d) The Club, Association o r person whom the agent o r intermediary
         claims to represent must confirm in writing both his plenary power
         to represent such a club, Association o r person and any agreements
         reached on their behalf. In cases of emergency, confirmation may
         be sent by cable and confirmed later in writing.
PERCENTAGE
   (e) The fees of the agent o r intermediary must not exceed 10% o f the
         sum which he procures for the Club o r National Association, plus
         the possible reimbursement of travelling expenses for one person.
         A ny written agreements stipulating a larger percentage shall be null
         and void.
   (f) The written agreements mentioned above must include a clause
         stipulating that both parties shall recognize that the agreement, in
         addition to the conditions contained therein, are subject to the
         overriding clauses and conditions laid down in Art. 10 of the
         Regulations o f the F.I.F.A.
   (g) During the period of an existing engagement, a player shall not be
        approached by an official of any other club in membership with
                                   APPENDIX                                289


          another National Association, with a view to inducing him to join a
          new club after his engagement has terminated.
 4. A ny person receiving remuneration for his services under contract with
    a National Association o r one o f its clubs (as coach for instance) shall
    not be entitled to simultaneously undertake any remunerated office
    whatsoever with another National Association.


       VII. Players Sent off the Field during International Matches or
                                 Tournaments
 Article 11
 SUSPENSIONS
 1. A player who has been sent off the field during an International or
     Inter-League match (Articles 6 and 8 of the Regulations) o r in an
     International T ournam ent is automatically suspended from taking part
     in International o r Inter-League matches o r in the matches of the
    T ournam ent concerned until such time as the Association to which the
    player belongs and/or the Disciplinary Com mittee of the Tournam ent
    concerned has taken appropriate penal action.
        In Tournam ents, the Disciplinary Com mittee may only suspend a
    player from taking part in the matches o f the T ournam ent. If more
    severe action is required the N ational Association to which the player
    belongs must take the appropriate action.
       In T ournam ents organized by F.I.F.A., such as the World C ham p­
    ionship, Olympic Football Tournam ents and others, the disciplinary
    measures shall be taken in accordance with the special regulations of
    these Tournam ents.
       F or each International Match and for each match in a T ournam ent
   the referee must furnish a report to the F.I.F.A. and to the National
   A ssociation in whose territory the match o r tournam ent was played,
   not later than 48 hours after the completion o f the match stating the
   reasons for any disciplinary action taken, including cautions and dis­
   missals.
       T he Association in question must send an exact copy to the A ssocia­
   tion to which the offending player belongs. The latter A ssociation shall
   be responsible for informing the Secretariat o f the F.I.F.A. and of the
   o ther A ssociation concerned of the action taken against the offending
   player.
2.    Each National A ssociation shall at once advise the National Associa­
     tion concerned o f the dismissal o f a player in an Inter-Club match (Art.
     9 of the Regulations). In the same way the Association to which the
290                              APPENDIX


   offending player belongs shall advise the other Association immedi­
   ately of the action taken against this player.
3. T he same disciplinary measures which apply to Inter-League matches
   shall also apply to matches between scratch-teams o r representative
   sides.

           VIII. Players Changing their National Association
Article 12
C E R T IF IC A T E O F T R A N S F E R
1. If a player (amateur, non-amateur, under contract o r licence, o r profes­
    sional) wishes to change his National Association he must inform it by
    registered letter of his desire to leave. The National Association with
   which he wishes to be registered, when informed of his intention, is
    alone entitled to ask for the certificate of transfer from the former
    Association. No Association may register such a player for one o f its
    clubs before being in possession of the transfer certificate.
2. The certificate of transfer shall be issued in duplicate and duly signed by
   the previous Association.
3. One copy shall be sent by registered letter to the Secretariat of the
   F.I.F.A . and the other to the new National Association.
4. The certificate of transfer shall contain the declaration that the holder
   of this certificate is free to play football in the area of another Associa­
   tion from the date shown on the certificate.
5. The issuing of this certificate shall imply on the part of the previous
   Association that all commitments of a financial nature, including the
   transfer fee where applicable, have been settled.
6. The Transfer Certificate must be unconditional but if in special cases
   separate agreements are established between the Clubs and/or National
   Associations concerned this must be stated on the Transfer Certificate
   by the words “ Separate Agreement” a copy of which has to be included.
7. If it is arranged to pay a transfer fee by installments, the club and the
   National Association to which the player belongs shall claim all neces­
   sary measures which can give the absolute guarantee of these payments
   by installments; without this, the respective transfer certificate cannot
   be issued.
8. The conditions laying down these payments by installments shall not be
   contained in a “ special convention or separate arrangement” which
   might be independent from the player’s transfer contract. They shall
   only be contained in the contract itself so that F.I.F.A. is exempted
                                  APPENDIX                                  291


    from every obligation in case o f total o r partial non-payment o f the
    installments.

Article 13
A M A T E U R PL A Y E R
1. If an am ateur player has not received his certificate of transfer, he
   cannot be registered by another Association until one year after he has
   informed his previous National Association by registered letter o f his
   desire to leave.
2. If the player maintains his request he must inform the new Association
   accordingly, this Association shall in turn inform the former A ssocia­
   tion by register letter.
3. The new Association must observe the stipulations o f A rt. 44 o f the
   F.I.F.A. Statutes and during the period o f one year mentioned above,
   the player may not play either for the new o r the former Association.

Article 14
P R O F E S S IO N A L P L A Y E R S
1. A professional player o r a non-am ateur player under contract o r licence
    may not leave his National Association so long as he is bound by his
    contract and by the Rules o f his club, his League and his National
    Associations, no m atter how harsh the term s o f his contract may be,
    provided that the contract is not in opposition to the Statutes and
    Regulations o f F.I.F.A. and the laws o f the countries concerned.
2. Unless cancellation o f a contract has been agreed in advance by both
   parties the new National Association may only ask for a certificate of
   transfer when the player has regained his freedom and fulfilled all the
   obligations o f his former contract, the regulations o f his club, his league
   and his National Association.
3. No club, League nor Association shall retain the services o f a player
   under contract without paying him the m inimum salary provided for in
   his contract.
4. The following rules shall be observed in dealings between clubs and
   professional players:
   (a) If the contract contains a clause which provides for breaking the
       agreement before expiration, each signatory shall have the right, in
       case o f such cancellation, to at least three months notice.
   (b) If a contract, with o r without a clause to terminate such contract
       before its actual expiration, contains a clause permitting the reten­
       tion o f the player after the expiration o f the contract, o r if such a
292                              APPENDIX


       clause is contained in the rules of the club, the League or its
       Association, the club wishing to invoke this retaining clause must
       inform the player at least one month before the expiration o f the
       contract. In the case o f a player having given notice to leave before
       the actual expiration, the club which intends to make use o f this
       retaining clause must inform the player not later than 15 days after
       receipt o f this notice given by the player.
   (c) A fter such time, and unless the player is the subject o f disciplinary
       action, the cancellation of contract by the player shall become valid,
       and his National Association shall send him his certificate of
       transfer.
5. As soon as a contract is registered with the national association con­
   cerned, the club is obliged to give the player a copy o f the signed
   contract.




Article 15
P R O V ISIO N A L C E R T IF IC A T E O F T R A N S F E R
   If the certificate o f transfer is not issued within a specified period, the
following procedure shall be observed:
1. Transfers o f players between Associations o f the same Continent:
SET T E R M
      If, after a period of 60 days the Association which a player wishes to
   leave has not issued him with a certificate o f transfer, the new A ssocia­
   tion may issue to the player a provisional transfer certificate.
2. Transfers of players between Associations o f different Continents:
      If, after a period o f 90 days the Association which a player wishes to
   leave has not issued him with a certificate o f transfer, the new Associa­
   tion may issue to the player a provisional transfer certificate.
3. In the two cases mentioned above, the provisional certificateof transfer
   shall become permanent one year after the date on which the new
   Association addressed its request to the former Association. In the
   event o f an unsatisfactory reply being received in the meantime (from
   the former Association), the provisional certificate shall be withdrawn
   immediately.
4. Art. 12-15 are not applicable to transactions between the four British
   Associations.
                                 APPENDIX
                                                                         293


 Article 16
 A P PE A L S
    If a player, after having changed his residence, is declared to be a
 professional or non-am ateur by his previous Association, the new Associ­
 ation may lodge an appeal against this decision with the Federation accord­
 ing to the procedure laid down in Art. 17.



Article 17
DISPUTES
1. Disputes arising from the transfer o f professional o r non-am ateur
   players between National Associations shall be decided by the Execu­
   tive Committee, upon report from the Players’ Status Committee.
2. While a dispute is being considered and before a final decision is
   reached, the player concerned shall not play for either his new o r his old
   Association.
3. In the event o f the decision being in favour o f the player, the Executive
   Committee shall make provision in its findings for the refund of any
   loss o f salary incurred by the player.



                          IX. Laws of the Game
Article 18
  The Laws of the Game are promulgated and altered by the International
Board, which consists o f twenty Members, sixteen o f whom are appointed
by the four British A ssociations, each o f which nominates four Members,
and four Members appointed by the Executive Committee o f F.I.F.A. (see
Art. 19 o f the Statutes). This Regulation cannot be changed except by the
unanim ous consent o f the Members of the Board.



Article 19
1. During the month following the meeting o f the International Board, the
   Federation shall inform all its National Associations o f any changes in
   the Laws of the Game issued by the International Board.
2. These changes in the Laws o f the G am e must be put into force by
   Associations during the m onth following receipt o f the notification.
3. Associations are empowered, however, to give effect to such changes
   immediately after they are issued by the International Board.
294                               APPENDIX


                                  X. Referees
Article 20
EX PEN SES
1. Referees of International Matches are entitled to the refund of travel­
   ling expenses (railway travel and sleeping accommodation 1st class; by
   boat 1st class and by plane tourist class o r 1st class, depending on the
   duration o f the journey). These expenses must be refunded to the
   referee on the day of the match by the National A ssociation organizing
   the match.
2. The hotel expenses and board are at the charge of the Association
   organizing the match.
D A IL Y A L L O W A N C E
3. T he referee is entitled to a daily allowance fixed from time to time by the
   Executive Committee after consultation with the Referees’ Committee
   in respect of the expenses on his journey (food, insurance and other
   expenses), which shall be paid to him for the actual days of his journey,
   on the day of the match, by the Association organizing the match.
R E F E R E E ’S R E P O R T
4. The official form of the Federation for the Referee’s Report must be
   handed to the referee by his Association when he is appointed. The
   referee must personally send this report duly completed within 48 hours
   after the match to the Secretariat of the F.I.F.A.:
  N.B. National Associations shall submit not later than 15th July in each year a list
       of the names of a number of referees as fixed by F.I.F.A. who, in their
       opinion, are suitable in every way to be appointed to International Matches,
       World Cups and Olympic Games Tournaments for a period of twelve
       months from the date of publication which will be on or about August 1st
       annually. No additions or alterations will be permitted after publication of
       the list unless the maximum number was not submitted in the first place or in
       case a referee shall cease to be available for appointments for any reason.
       Alterations and additions to the list will not be acceptable after January 1st
       in each year on which date National Associations will be notified of any
       changes.




                         XI. Matters not Provided for
 Article 21
 PO W E RS
   A ny matters not provided for in these Regulations shall be decided by
 the Executive Committee.
                                APPENDIX                                295


                            XII. Interpretation
Article 22
  In the event of any differences of interpretation in regard to the English,
French, Spanish o r German text, the English text shall be authoritative.
Article 23
   These Regulations have been adopted by the Extraordinary Congress of
the 14th/15th November, 1953, in Paris, and altered by subsequent C on­
gresses. The Regulations and alterations shall come into force as laid down
in A rt. 17 of the Statutes.

                 STATUTES OF THE F.I.F.A.
(Approved and adopted by Congress 1961 and altered by subsequent
                         Congresses.)

Article 41
F O R B ID D E N R E L A T IO N S H IP
1. Affiliated Associations and their clubs shall not be permitted to play
   matches against o r have sporting relationship with Associations, o r
   their clubs, not in membership with F.I.F.A. w ithout the consent of the
   Executive Committee of the Federation.
2. Affiliated A ssociations and their clubs shall not be permitted to play
   matches against teams consisting of players who do not belong exclu­
   sively to a club o r League affiliated to a National Association.
3. National A ssociations shall not form themselves into groups without
   the special consent o f the Federation.
4. Members of the Federation may not play matches on the territory of
   another National Association without the consent of such A ssociation.
296                             APPENDIX


Article 42
M E M B E R S H IP W IT H A N O T H E R N A T IO N A L A SSO C IA TIO N
  Associations, Leagues o r clubs established within the territory of a
National Association affiliated to the Federation shall not be permitted to
become members of another National A ssociation except with the permis­
sion of the former Association and the confirmation of the Federation.

Article 43
C O U N T R Y W IT H O U T F.I.F.A. M E M B E R SH IP
  Associations or clubs established in a territory o r country where there is
no A ssociation affiliated to the Federation shall not become members of a
National Association in membership with the Federation without the
special consent of the Federation.



                               XII. Disputes
Article 48
A R B IT R A T IO N T R IB U N A L
1. National Associations, clubs o r members of clubs shall not be permit­
   ted to bring before a Court of Justice disputes with the Federation or
   other Associations, clubs o r members of clubs and they must agree to
   submit any such disputes to an A rbitration Tribunal appointed by
   common consent.
 2. Should the laws o f a country entitle the National Association concerned
    and its clubs and their members to appeal to a Court of Law, the
    National Association must insert a clause in its Statutes, by which it
    freely renounces, along with its clubs and their members, the right to
    take a dispute before the Courts, and undertakes to accept the decisions
    o f the arbitrators selected.
 P O W E R S O F E X E C U T IV E C O M M IT TE E
 3. In the event o f a disagreement between two o r several Associations, the
     Executive Committee shall have the right to take a decision, if the
     Associations concerned are unable to agree upon the choice of an
     arbitrator. This decision shall be final and binding upon the Associa­
     tions concerned.
 4. National Associations must adhere strictly to the decisions of the
    Federation o r the arbitrators selected by it, and where these decisions
    concern a club, a Regional Association o r a League, the respective
    National Association must take the necessary steps to ensure that the
    decisions are observed.
                                 APPENDIX                                 297


5. A ssociations violating any one o f the clauses o f this Article shall be
   expelled from the Federation, in conformity with the provisions of Art.
   50, para. 1, clauses (b) and (c).
6. Disputes regarding the transfer of players (Art. 16 o f the Regulations)
   o r the registration of players (Art. 17 o f the Regulations) shall be
   decided by the Executive Com mittee on the basis of a report submitted
   by the Players’ Status Committee.

                 TRANSFER OF PLAYERS OVERSEAS
   The Football Association, over the past years, has been consulted by
many players, who having emigrated to overseas countries, primarily to
play football, have returned to this country and have wished to resume
playing here. They have been unable to do so because the Club for which
they have been playing overseas has refused to release them and
consequently they have been unable to receive an International Clearance
Certificate from the National Association concerned, which Certificate is
essential before The Football Association may give the player permission
to resume playing in England.
   The International Clearance Certificate is a F.I.F.A. recognised
document which governs the transfer o f players from one country to
another. W ithout such a Certificate no English player may play overseas
and no foreign player may play in England.
   Players are frequently unaware o f these Regulations and sometimes
enter into agreements or make arrangements for leaving one country to
play football in another which subsequently cannot be confirmed, thereby
 causing distress and inconvenience. It is essential, therefore, that the widest
 publicity be given to this Memorandum. The problem is diverse as
difficulties can arise which vary considerably but whatever the playing
status o f the individual, an International Clearance Certificate is required.
      A player may go overseas on payment of a transfer fee, or on a free
transfer. On arrival overseas as a player not under written contract he may
become a player under written contract. Because values are different
overseas from what they are in this country, he may have a transfer fee
placed on his head by his overseas Club; indeed he may be transferred for
comparatively large sums o f money within the overseas territory. When he
returns to this country it is not usual for any Club to be prepared to pay the
transfer fee which the overseas Club has put on him as a condition o f his
transfer. The experience of The Football Association is that the player can
be literally out o f work as a footballer for a long period o f time and maybe
the player left this country without anybody paying a penny for his
services.
298                            APPENDIX


   It is suggested that when a player is transferred to an overseas Club
without any payment of a fee, it is clearly a condition of transfer and so
stated on a “ Separate Agreement” on the International Clearance
Certificate that the transfer is conditional on the individual being free to
return to this country, subject to his observing any contractual arrange­
ments in respect o f his services overseas, without any transfer fee being
required from any Club overseas.
   Emphasis is placed on the phrase ‘subject to his observing any
contractual arrangements in respect o f his services overseas’. We have
found that a player having gone overseas and having changed his Club
overseas on payment of a fee, has entered into a contract with his Club
which virtually binds him to the Club and makes it impossible to return to
this country. Whilst The Football Association can safeguard his position
when he first leaves this country by a suitable “ Separate Agreement” on
the International Clearance Certificate, it cannot preserve that position if,
and when, he changes his Club within the overseas territory. The player
should ensure himself that his right to return to this country without let or
hindrance, if he so desires, is preserved.
   Clubs should also be aware o f the dangers in permitting players to go
overseas to play football during the close season in England. If a Club
wishes to regain its player after the period o f service overseas, it must
clearly make it a condition o f the release o f the player to a Club that the
Club guarantees to return the player on request and that the player does so
return. It would be an extra safeguard to the Club to obtain the signature of
the player to a statement making it quite clear that he understands that the
arrangement is temporary and that he will return to his Club when
requested to do so. A specimen agreement is available from The
Association.
   In addition it is pointed out that it is not possible for an International
Clearance Certificate to be issued on behalf o f a player who is currently
registered under written contract for a Club with this Association. Before
the International Clearance Certificate may be issued it is necessary for
any such registration to be cancelled by mutual consent on the appropriate
form as provided for under the Rules of The Association.
   In accordance with the Regulations of F.I.F.A . dealing with Players
changing their National Association it m ust be noted that in the event of a
Player coming to E ngland and wishing to play football who previously
played under the jurisdiction of another National Association (not includ­
ing Scotland, Northern Ireland and Wales) it is necessary for The Football
Association to receive an International Clearance Certificate issued on his
behalf by the former National Association before he may play for any Club
                                      a p p e n d ix
                                                                                299


 in this country. It is pointed out that the Regulations apply both to Players
 under written contract and those not under written contract and to all
 affiliated Clubs at all levels of the game.
